Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: piano\\ \tt RIGHT: jacket\\ \tt TOP: cat\\ \tt BOTTOM: elephant\\ \tt CENTER: bees\\ \tt NORTHWEST: bolt\\ \tt NORTHEAST: frying pan\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: apples\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: bronzer\\ \tt HERE: lily\\ \tt THERE: pencil sharpener\\ \tt NOWHERE: shirt\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: bluebell\\ \tt INSIDE: mango\\ \tt OUTSIDE: passion fruit\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   }
